#   PB_RxSecAuth            — Security authentication

#   PB_RxDisconnectInfo     — Disconnect notification
#   PB_RxPipeRoleChange     — Dynamic BLE pipe role switching
#   PB_RxTimeSyncInfo       — Time synchronization

#   PB_RxRestoreFactory     — Factory reset
#

#   PB_RxEvenAICtrl         — AI control (type 1)
